We r lucky with injuries and suddenly everyone is saying we have the strongest, deepest squad.  And Origi is a big part of that.  NO clubs in world football can ever claim to have a 6th forward with such qualities as Origi. And then we have Minamino and Elliot and Gordon too, to boot, and other youngsters-- some who r on loan.  But Origi is the secret ingredient for our recent surges and achievements and it goes without saying.  He and Minamino have played very important roles earlier in this season in Cup games. But I know there will be naysayers esp because of the age factor.  I do believe your team of coaches and recruits have done an excellent job, so if those 2 r impossible, no prob.  But please...Origi is 27.  No excuse there. I have already said how he can get just that few extra games he craves and deserves.   That will really work in favour of more success and less injuries for Liverpool.

I love you. Glad you will stay for another two years. Glad if you stay in Liveprool forever. But I'm writing this for a very simple reason; first and foremost, as a note-reminder towards myself.   If you decided to leave in 2024, which I had thought about it a lot, I had friends ask me about it (knowing my unending love towards the club but, more importantly, seeing themselves that "match made in heaven" of  Liverpool and you) - I would be fine with it. Really. You have given me so much joy;  and sometimes during the most difficult personal times. But times like the ones we are correctly living in aren't personally difficult. They are difficult for all of us, in so many different ways. The whole world has changed. And you, and this team, are the only constant of beauty- or, if that sounds like a hyperbole, one of the very few.  I don't know when every fan fell in love with Liverpool. It depends on their age. For me, it was during the Gerrard years,a bit earlier. I have experienced real lows for this team, with this team. I have cried my eyes out seeing this team crumble, fall, underperform, playing appalling football at times. I have cried all half-time long in Istanbul final, and rejoiced at the end. The word "rejoice" doesn't really say what I felt that night. Neither I can find a word for Gerrard's equalizer against West Ham. I have seen great players, loved them with passion, cried when they left.  I have never seen anyone being the living embodiment of what every true fan of Liveprool didn't even dare to dream. You are that embodiment. All us fans owe great moments; moments we couldn't even imagine before you came.  You really, really make a difference. Yes, it's "just football". But you are responsible for making it something more than that. Liverpool has become a fountain of joy, a stream of happiness, an ocean of true,original positivity. Again, thank you from the bottom of my heart. I love you. You have given everything and then some. If you decided to leave, I would be glad we had you. I could never feel greedy and ask for more. But I'm as glad as I can be that decided to stay.
